## ğŸ¯ Recommended Navigation Structure:

### **Home Tab** (What you're designing):
- AI Pick of the Day card
- League filters (EPL, Championship, etc.)
- Date filters (Today, Tomorrow, Weekend)
- Match cards with checkboxes + analyze button
- Bottom action bar when matches selected

### **Bet Slips Tab:**
- Library of saved parlays
- Filter: Active, Won, Lost
- Each slip shows: odds, confidence, date
- Tap to view full analysis
- Options: Edit, Delete, Share

### **Profile Tab:**
- User info (if accounts later)
- Settings (odds format, notifications)
- About app
- Help/FAQ
- Version info

GREAT QUESTION! This is actually a key thing to understand about Cursor (and AI coding assistants in general).

ğŸ¯ SHORT ANSWER:
Cursor understands DESIGN PATTERNS, not specific content.
You can show it:

"Man City vs Liverpool" in your design
But it will apply the same layout to "Arsenal vs Chelsea" in the real app

The content doesn't need to match - the STRUCTURE does.

ğŸ“‹ How Cursor Actually Works:
What Cursor Sees:
[Your Figma Screenshot]

Cursor interprets:
1. There's a card with a match header
2. Below that: League Position section
3. Below that: Recent Form (W/L/D circles)
4. Below that: Injuries list
5. Below that: Head-to-Head text
6. Below that: Betting Angles bullets

Pattern understood âœ…
What Cursor Builds:
javascript// Cursor creates a COMPONENT that works for ANY match

function MatchBreakdown({ match }) {
  return (
    <Card>
      <Header>{match.homeTeam} vs {match.awayTeam}</Header>
      <Time>{match.time}</Time>
      
      <Section icon="ğŸ“Š">
        <Title>LEAGUE POSITION</Title>
        <Text>{match.homeTeam} {match.homePosition} vs {match.awayTeam} {match.awayPosition}</Text>
      </Section>
      
      <Section icon="ğŸ“ˆ">
        <Title>RECENT FORM</Title>
        <FormDots team1={match.homeForm} team2={match.awayForm} />
      </Section>
      
      <Section icon="ğŸ¤•">
        <Title>INJURIES & SUSPENSIONS</Title>
        <InjuryList team1={match.homeInjuries} team2={match.awayInjuries} />
      </Section>
      
      {/* etc... */}
    </Card>
  )
}
```

**Then it fetches REAL match data from APIs and populates the component!**

## âœ… What You NEED to Show Cursor:

### **1. Visual Structure** â­ CRITICAL
- Card layout
- Section order
- Spacing, padding
- Typography (sizes, weights)
- Colors, borders
- Icons placement

### **2. Data Types** â­ IMPORTANT
- "This shows team names"
- "This shows W/L/D form"
- "This shows injury list"
- "This shows odds"

### **3. Interaction Patterns** â­ IMPORTANT
- "Card expands when tapped"
- "Chevron rotates up when expanded"
- "Shows 5 most recent form results"

---

## âŒ What You DON'T Need to Match:

### **1. Specific Team Names**
```
Design shows: "Man City vs Liverpool"
Real app shows: "Arsenal vs Chelsea"
Cursor: âœ… No problem! Same layout, different data
```

### **2. Exact Numbers**
```
Design shows: "2nd (16pts) vs 3rd (15pts)"
Real app shows: "1st (20pts) vs 8th (10pts)"
Cursor: âœ… No problem! Same format, different numbers
```

### **3. Injury Names**
```
Design shows: "Alisson OUT (hamstring)"
Real app shows: "Salah doubtful (illness)"
Cursor: âœ… No problem! Same injury list format
```

### **4. Form Patterns**
```
Design shows: W-W-D-W-W
Real app shows: L-L-W-D-L
Cursor: âœ… No problem! Same W/L/D circles, different pattern

ğŸ¨ What Your Design TEACHES Cursor:
Looking at your expanded match breakdown:
Cursor Learns:

âœ… "Ah, there's a section called LEAGUE POSITION with team standings"
âœ… "Recent form shows 5 colored circles (green W, red L, gray D)"
âœ… "Injuries section lists players with their injury type in parentheses"
âœ… "HEAD-TO-HEAD shows historical meeting data"
âœ… "BETTING ANGLES shows 3 bullet points with betting recommendations"
âœ… "Sections have icons and ALL CAPS headers"
âœ… "Chevron on right indicates expandable"

Then Cursor Builds:
javascript// Component that works for ANY match
<MatchCard 
  homeTeam={apiData.homeTeam}
  awayTeam={apiData.awayTeam}
  homePosition={apiData.standings.home}
  awayPosition={apiData.standings.away}
  homeForm={apiData.form.home}  // Array: ['W','W','D','W','W']
  awayForm={apiData.form.away}   // Array: ['W','L','W','W','L']
  injuries={apiData.injuries}     // Array of injury objects
  h2h={apiData.headToHead}        // H2H text
  bettingAngles={aiGenerated}     // AI-generated recommendations
/>
```

âœ… Visual design (layout, colors, spacing)

What Cursor Doesn't Need:

âŒ Actual API responses in Figma

You design with example data (Man City vs Liverpool)

### 2. **"Based on form, injuries, and betting value"**

Not critical either way!

### 3. **Mobile Scrolling**

But honestly, the natural scroll is fine for MVP!

### 4. **Expanded Match - Slight Inconsistency**
In your expanded match, you show:
```
Man United: W W D W W
Man City: W L W W L
```

But earlier you had team logos next to form. 

**Keep it consistent with your single match analysis:**
```
ğŸ”´ Man United: W W D W W
ğŸ”µ Man City:   W L W W L
Small detail, but consistency matters!

5. "Add to Bet Slip" vs "Select This Parlay"
You went with "Add to Bet Slip" - perfect choice!
Much clearer than "Select This Parlay". Users know exactly what happens.

6. Sticky Bottom Action?
Question: When user taps "Add to Bet Slip" on a parlay, what happens?
Options:
Option A: Goes to Bet Slip immediately

User taps button
Navigates to Bet Slips tab
Parlay is loaded and ready

Option B: Adds to slip, shows confirmation

User taps button
Toast notification: "Added to Bet Slip âœ“"
Can add multiple parlays
Bottom nav badge shows count (Bet Slips [2])

Option C: Bottom bar appears

User taps "Add to Bet Slip"
Floating bar appears at bottom: "1 parlay added | View Bet Slip â†’"
Can continue browsing or go to bet slip

My recommendation: Option B (toast + badge)

Least disruptive
Clear feedback
Allows comparing multiple parlays before deciding


ğŸ”§ Technical Questions for Building:
1. Match Expansion Logic
When user taps a match card, should:

Only one match expand at a time (others collapse)?
OR multiple matches can be expanded simultaneously?

My vote: One at a time (cleaner, less scrolling)

2. Parlay Selection
Can users:

Add one parlay to bet slip?
OR add multiple parlays to compare?

My vote: Multiple parlays (power users want to compare)

3. Injury Data Source
Where will injuries come from?

API-Football (includes injuries) âœ…
Web scraping (Premier Injuries, TransferMarkt)
Manual updates (not scalable)

My vote: Start with API-Football, supplement with scraping if needed

## 3. ğŸ¨ Should You Build Design System with Tokens/Variables?

**SHORT ANSWER: Not necessary for Cursor, but helpful for YOU.**

### **Reality Check:**

**Cursor doesn't read Figma tokens/variables.** When you show Cursor a screenshot, it sees:
- "This text is light blue"
- "This button has rounded corners"
- "This card has 16px padding"

It does NOT see:
- "This uses $color-primary-500 token"
- "This uses $spacing-md variable"

### **But Design Tokens ARE Valuable For:**

âœ… **Your own consistency** - Making updates easier
âœ… **Handoff documentation** - If you ever hire a developer
âœ… **Professional portfolio** - Shows you know design systems

### **My Recommendation:**

**Basic tokens (15-20 minutes):**
```
Colors:
- Primary: #0EA5E9
- Background: #0f172a
- Card: #1e293b
- Text Primary: #ffffff
- Text Secondary: #94a3b8
- Success: #22c55e
- Warning: #f59e0b
- Error: #ef4444

Spacing:
- XS: 4px
- S: 8px
- M: 16px
- L: 24px
- XL: 32px

Typography:
- Heading: SF Pro Display, 24px, Bold
- Body: SF Pro Text, 16px, Regular
- Small: SF Pro Text, 14px, Regular
```

**Advanced system (2-3 hours):**
- Semantic tokens (--color-button-primary, --color-card-background)
- Component variants
- Responsive breakpoints
- Dark mode variations (you're already dark!)

**My vote:** Basic tokens only. Write them in a separate doc, share with Cursor when building.

## 5. ğŸ¤– Figma Make Prompts

### **Prompt 1: Betslips Library Screen**
```
Design a mobile betting app screen called "My Betslips" in dark mode 
with these specifications:

DESIGN SYSTEM:
- Background: Dark navy (#0f172a)
- Cards: Slate (#1e293b)
- Primary action: Electric blue (#0EA5E9)
- Text primary: White
- Text secondary: Light gray (#94a3b8)
- Success: Green (#22c55e)
- Font: SF Pro (iOS native)

LAYOUT:

TOP SECTION:
- "My Betslips" header (24px, bold, centered)
- Filter tabs below header (pill-style buttons):
  [Active] [Saved] [Won] [Lost]
- Active tab: blue background, others: dark gray

BETSLIP CARDS (scrollable list):
Each card shows:
- Parlay name: "3-Leg Safest Parlay" (18px, bold)
- Teams: "Man City + Liverpool + Chelsea" (14px, medium)
- Odds: "4.85x" (large, blue, top-right)
- Confidence badge: "72% AI" (small, top-left)
- Status badge: "Active" (green) or "Won" (green with âœ“) or "Lost" (red)
- Date: "Saved: Oct 30, 3:42 PM" (small, gray)
- Divider line between cards

EMPTY STATE (when no betslips):
- Icon: Empty folder or betting slip icon (gray)
- Text: "No betslips yet"
- Subtext: "Create a parlay to get started"
- Button: "Analyze Matches" (blue)

BOTTOM:
- Navigation bar with 3 tabs:
  Home | Betslips (active/blue) | Profile

INTERACTION HINTS:
- Cards should look tappable (subtle shadow)
- "Active" betslips have slightly brighter appearance
- Filter tabs show count: "Active (3)" if there are 3 active slips

AVOID:
- Casino-style graphics
- Cluttered layouts
- Tiny text
- Overwhelming colors

Make it clean, professional, and easy to scan.
```

### **Prompt 2: Loading State**
```
Design a mobile app loading screen in dark mode for a sports 
betting AI analysis app:

DESIGN SYSTEM:
- Background: Dark navy (#0f172a)
- Primary: Electric blue (#0EA5E9)
- Text: White and light gray
- Font: SF Pro

LAYOUT:
- Centered vertically and horizontally
- Robot/AI icon at top (simple, blue)
- Loading spinner below icon (blue, rotating)
- Main text: "Analyzing Matches..." (20px, white, bold)
- Subtext: "Crunching 10,000+ data points across 3 matches" (14px, gray)
- Progress indicator (optional): "2 of 3 matches analyzed"

STYLE:
- Minimal and clean
- Professional, not playful
- Subtle animation hint (spinner, pulse)
- Lots of breathing room

VARIATIONS NEEDED:
1. General loading: "Analyzing Matches..."
2. Fetching odds: "Loading Latest Odds..."
3. AI thinking: "Generating Recommendations..."

Keep it simple and professional.
```

### **Prompt 3: Error State**
```
Design a mobile app error screen in dark mode for a sports 
betting analysis app:

DESIGN SYSTEM:
- Background: Dark navy (#0f172a)
- Error color: Soft red (#ef4444)
- Button: Electric blue (#0EA5E9)
- Text: White and light gray
- Font: SF Pro

LAYOUT:
- Centered vertically and horizontally
- Warning icon at top (âš ï¸ or alert symbol, soft red)
- Main text: "Unable to Load Matches" (20px, white, bold)
- Subtext: "Check your internet connection and try again" (14px, gray)
- Retry button: "Retry" (blue, rounded)
- Secondary link: "Contact Support" (14px, underlined, gray)

VARIATIONS NEEDED:
1. Network error: "Unable to Load Matches" + internet check
2. API error: "Something Went Wrong" + "We're looking into it"
3. No matches: "No Matches Available" + "Check back soon"

STYLE:
- Calm and helpful (not alarming)
- Clear action path (retry button)
- Professional, not apologetic
- Breathing room around elements

AVOID:
- Scary error messages
- Technical jargon
- Red everywhere (just accent)
- Blame on user
```

Or shall we discuss the Cursor build strategy?RetryPTQuestion about the my betting slips screen - I suppose it would be good to see which bets worked or not, but that wont be automated. Because it won't be connected like that. The user would need to say each time whether they were successful or not. What do you think? Have that feature - I don't know whether it would work against the app as confirming the negative if the user loses a few bets in a rowWeighed manual tracking's motivational risks against transparency benefits.This is a REALLY insightful question about psychology, user experience, and product design. Let me think through this carefully.
The user is asking about tracking bet outcomes (Won/Lost) in the betslip library, and raises two key concerns:

Manual tracking - Since the app isn't connected to sportsbooks, users would have to manually mark bets as won/lost
Psychological impact - Seeing a string of losses might demotivate users and make them abandon the app

This is actually a sophisticated product design question that involves:

User psychology and behavioral design
Gambling harm reduction
Product retention vs transparency
Feature prioritization for MVP

Let me think about different approaches:
Arguments FOR tracking wins/losses:

Helps users learn what strategies work
Shows ROI and effectiveness
Professional bettors want this data
Demonstrates app value (if AI picks are winning)
Accountability and learning

Arguments AGAINST tracking:

Manual input is friction
Seeing losses can be demotivating
Gambling apps often hide losses to keep people playing (but that's predatory)
Not automated = low adoption
Could highlight when AI predictions are wrong

Middle ground options:

Optional tracking (users can opt-in)
Only show wins (hide losses) - but that's deceptive
Focus on "saved" vs "placed" rather than won/lost
Track predictions vs outcomes separately from user's actual bets
Use positive framing ("Learning insights" vs "You lost")

I think the user is right to be concerned. This is a delicate balance between:

Being helpful and transparent
Not demotivating users
Not being predatory (hiding losses)
Keeping the app focused on analysis, not tracking

Let me give them a comprehensive answer with multiple options and my honest recommendation.EXCELLENT question! This is actually a really nuanced product design challenge that involves psychology, ethics, and UX. Let me break this down:

ğŸ¯ The Core Problem:
Manual tracking = friction + potential negativity spiral
You're right to be concerned about:

User friction - Manually updating each bet outcome is tedious
Loss aversion - Seeing "Lost, Lost, Lost" can trigger abandonment
Blame the tool - Users might blame your app for their losses
Demotivation - String of red "Lost" badges = depressing experience


ğŸ’­ The Psychology:
Gambling apps face this dilemma:

Predatory approach: Hide losses, emphasize wins (keep users gambling)
Responsible approach: Show reality, but risk demotivating users
Your app: Analysis tool, not sportsbook - different responsibility

Key insight: Your app's value is in the analysis quality, not bet outcomes.

ğŸ¨ Design Options (Ranked):
OPTION 1: Focus on "Analysis Tracking" Not "Bet Tracking" â­ RECOMMENDED
Instead of:
Status: Won âœ… / Lost âŒ
```

**Show:**
```
Created: Oct 30, 2024
AI Prediction: 72% confidence
Status: [Track Outcome â†’] (optional)
```

**Benefits:**
- Emphasizes the analysis, not gambling outcome
- Removes pressure to track losses
- Still allows tracking for those who want it
- Psychologically frames app as research tool

**UI:**
```

### **OPTION 2: Positive Framing Only** (Controversial but Effective)

**Only track wins, not losses:**
```
Filter tabs: [All] [Saved] [Wins ğŸ‰]

No "Lost" tab
```

**When user marks as won:**
```
Status: Won âœ… +$62 profit
```

**When user marks as lost:**
```
Status: Archived
(No negative messaging)
```

**Benefits:**
- Reduces demotivation
- Celebrates successes
- Still shows reality (absence of wins = didn't win)
- Less guilt-inducing

**Concerns:**
- Could be seen as deceptive
- Not helpful for serious bettors who want honest tracking
- Ethically questionable

**My take:** This is what consumer gambling apps do, but feels manipulative for an "intelligence" app.

## ğŸ¯ My Honest Recommendation:

### **For MVP: Option 4 (No outcome tracking)**

**Why:**
1. **Simplest to build** - No complex tracking logic
2. **Zero ethical concerns** - Not hiding losses, not pressuring tracking
3. **Focuses on your core value** - Analysis quality, not gambling outcomes
4. **Less liability** - Not responsible for user's betting results
5. **Ship faster** - Get to market, learn what users actually want

**Your betslip library shows:**
- Saved parlays
- AI confidence
- When created
- Ability to re-analyze if matches haven't happened yet

**That's it. Clean, simple, valuable.**

---

### **For V2: Option 3 (Learning-focused tracking)**

**Once you have users, add:**
- Optional outcome tracking
- AI post-match analysis ("Why this won/lost")
- Pattern insights ("You're 75% accurate on EPL")
- Improvement suggestions

**This becomes a learning tool, not just a tracking tool.**

---

## ğŸ“Š What Competitors Do:

**Action Network:**
- Tracks wins/losses prominently
- Shows P/L (profit/loss)
- But they're targeting serious bettors who want honesty

**FanDuel/DraftKings:**
- Track everything automatically (they process bets)
- Show brutal honesty (your balance is $0)
- But they have regulatory requirements

**BetIQ/Rithmm:**
- Focus on pick accuracy, not user outcomes
- "Our model is 68% accurate" not "you lost money"
- Smart positioning

**Your opportunity:** Be more like BetIQ - focus on analysis quality, not gambling outcomes.

---

**Key elements:**
- âœ… Shows what betslip is
- âœ… Shows AI confidence (your value prop)

## ğŸ’¡ Alternative: "Analysis History" Not "Bet History"

**Reframe the entire section:**

Instead of: "My Betslips"
Use: "My Analyses" or "Saved Analyses"

**This positions your app as:**
- Research tool âœ…
- Intelligence platform âœ…
- Decision support âœ…

**NOT as:**
- Bet tracker âŒ
- Gambling ledger âŒ
- Win/loss recorder âŒ

**This is psychologically smarter positioning.**

---

## ğŸš¨ The Ethical Consideration:

**You're right to think about this carefully.**

**Bad approaches:**
- Hiding losses to keep users gambling (predatory)
- Pressuring users to track (creates guilt)
- Showing only wins (deceptive)

**Good approaches:**
- Optional tracking (user choice)
- Learning-focused (educational)
- No tracking for MVP (simple, honest)

**Your app should help people make INFORMED decisions, not gamble more.**

---

## ğŸ“‹ My Final Recommendation:

### **MVP (Launch):**
```
Betslip Library with:
- [Active] [Saved] tabs only
- No outcome tracking
- Focus on analysis quality
- Simple: View, Share, Delete actions
```

### **V1.5 (3 months post-launch):**
```
Add OPTIONAL outcome tracking:
- "Track result?" button (not required)
- If user tracks, show learning insights
- Aggregate stats: "AI predictions 68% accurate"
- Never shame users for losses
```

### **V2 (6 months post-launch):**
```
Advanced insights:
- Pattern recognition ("You're better at EPL than La Liga")
- AI improvement suggestions
- Comparative analysis ("This parlay type is your strongest")
- Educational content based on their history
```

ğŸ¯ Bottom Line:
You're absolutely right to be concerned. Manual loss tracking in a betting app can:

Demotivate users
Create negative associations with your app
Increase abandonment
Feel predatory if not handled carefully

Best approach for MVP:

txtPARLAYS FOR DAYS - DESIGN SYSTEM

Colors:
- Primary: #0EA5E9 (Electric Blue)

- Card: #1e293b (Slate)

- H1 (Screen Titles): 24px, Bold, White
- H2 (Section Headers): 18px, Bold, White
- Body: 16px, Regular, White
- Small (Timestamps): 14px, Regular, Gray
- Tiny (Labels): 12px, Regular, Gray
- Font: SF Pro (system default)

Spacing:
- Card padding: 16px
- Section spacing: 24px
- Element spacing: 8px
- Screen margins: 16px

Components:
- Match cards: Dark slate, 12px rounded corners
- Buttons: Blue, 8px rounded, bold text
- Badges: Small, rounded, colored backgrounds
- Form dots: 24px circles (W=green, L=red, D=gray)

- Shows teams, time, odds, league logo

// Check if first time user
if (isFirstTimeUser()) {
  // Show onboarding (if you built it)
  showOnboarding();

  setTimeout(() => {
    showTooltip({
      target: '.analyze-button',
      message: 'Tap for AI analysis',
      position: 'bottom-left'
    });
  }, 500);
  
  // Mark as seen
  localStorage.setItem('tooltipSeen', 'true');
}
```

ğŸ“ Part 4: Create Essential Documents
Document 1: design-system.md (15 minutes)
Create a simple text file:
markdown# Parlays for Days - Design System

## Colors
- **Primary Blue**: #0EA5E9
- **Background**: #0f172a
- **Card Background**: #1e293b
- **Card Background Selected**: #1e3a5f (slightly lighter)
- **Text Primary**: #ffffff
- **Text Secondary**: #94a3b8
- **Success Green**: #22c55e
- **Warning Amber**: #f59e0b
- **Error Red**: #ef4444

## Typography
- **Font Family**: SF Pro Display (system default)
- **Screen Title**: 24px, Bold, White
- **Section Header**: 18px, Bold, White
- **Body Text**: 16px, Regular, White
- **Small Text**: 14px, Regular, Gray (#94a3b8)
- **Tiny Text**: 12px, Regular, Gray

## Spacing
- **Screen padding**: 16px
- **Card padding**: 16px
- **Card margin**: 12px between cards
- **Section spacing**: 24px between sections
- **Element spacing**: 8px between related elements

## Border Radius
- **Cards**: 12px
- **Buttons**: 8px
- **Badges**: 6px
- **Pills (filters)**: 20px

## Components

### Match Card
- Dark slate background (#1e293b)
- 12px rounded corners
- Team logos: 32px
- Odds on right: 16px, medium weight
- League icon top-left: 24px
- Analyze button (logo) top-right: 32px
- Checkbox top-left: 20px

### Bottom Navigation
- 3 tabs: Home, Betslips, Profile
- Active: Blue icon + text (#0EA5E9)
- Inactive: Gray (#64748b)
- Height: 80px
- Icons: 24px

### Buttons
- **Primary**: Blue background, white text, 8px radius
- **Height**: 48px
- **Padding**: 16px horizontal
- **Font**: 16px, Bold

### Form Indicator (W/L/D)
- Circles: 24px diameter
- Win: Green (#22c55e)
- Loss: Red (#ef4444)
- Draw: Gray (#64748b)
- 4px spacing between circles

Document 2: component-notes.md (10 minutes)
markdown# Component Behaviors

## Match Card
- **Default state**: Gray border
- **Selected state**: Blue border (#0EA5E9), checkbox checked
- **Hover state**: Slight brightness increase
- **Analyze button**: Tap opens single match analysis screen

## Floating "Analyze Parlay" Button
- **Appears**: When 2+ matches selected
- **Text**: "X matches selected | Analyze Parlay â†’"
- **Position**: Fixed bottom, above nav bar
- **Action**: Takes to Parlay Analysis screen

## Bottom Navigation
- **Home**: Shows match list
- **Betslips**: Shows saved parlays (Active/Saved tabs)
- **Profile**: Shows settings
- **Active indicator**: Blue background pill behind active tab

## Tooltips
- **First load**: Show "Tap for AI analysis" pointing to logo
- **Dismiss**: Tap anywhere or 3 seconds
- **Never show again**: Store in localStorage

## AI Pick of the Day
- **Location**: Top of home screen
- **Updates**: Daily at midnight
- **Tappable**: Opens full parlay analysis for that pick
- **Design**: Blue card, crown icon, team names + odds + confidence

Document 3: api-requirements.md (5 minutes)
markdown# API Requirements

## Data Needed

### Match Data
- Team names
- Team logos
- League info
- Match time
- Current odds (home/away/draw)
- Source: The Odds API + API-Football

### Analysis Data (from AI)
- Current form (last 5 results W/L/D)
- Injuries and suspensions
- Head-to-head history
- League position
- Betting angles (recommended bets)
- AI confidence percentage
- Source: Claude API analyzing web data

### Real-time Updates
- Lineup confirmations
- Late injuries
- Odds changes

## API Endpoints Needed
1. Get today's matches by league
2. Get match details by ID
3. Get team form and stats
4. Get injuries
5. Trigger AI analysis for match(es)
```

â”œâ”€â”€ Type: Primary | Secondary | Ghost | Destructive
â”œâ”€â”€ Size: Large | Medium | Small
â”œâ”€â”€ Icon: None | Left | Right
â””â”€â”€ State: Default | Hover | Disabled | Loading

## ğŸ“ Exact Specs for Each Size:

### **LARGE** (Full-width CTAs, main actions)
```
Height: 48px
Padding: 16px horizontal
Font: 16px, Bold
Border radius: 8px or 12px (your choice - I'd go with 12px for softer look)
Min-width: None (stretches to container)
```

**Use cases:**
- Bottom of forms
- Empty states ("Analyze Matches")
- Modal primary actions

---

### **MEDIUM** (Normal buttons, inline actions)
```
Height: 40px
Padding: 16px horizontal
Font: 14px, Bold (or 16px Medium)
Border radius: 8px
Min-width: 120px
```

**Use cases:**
- "Add to Betslip"
- "Analyze Parlay" (with arrow)
- Cards actions
- Floating button

---

### **SMALL** (Compact areas, tags, chips)
```
Height: 32px
Padding: 12px horizontal
Font: 14px, Medium
Border radius: 6px
Min-width: 80px
```

**Use cases:**
- Inline actions in lists
- Modal secondary actions
- Filters (though yours use pills, which is different)

---

## ğŸ¨ Color Reference:
```
Primary:
- Background: #0EA5E9
- Hover: #0284c7 (slightly darker)
- Pressed: #0369a1 (even darker)
- Disabled: #0EA5E9 at 40% opacity

Secondary:
- Background: #334155
- Hover: #475569 (lighter slate)
- Pressed: #1e293b (darker)
- Disabled: #334155 at 40% opacity

Ghost:
- Background: Transparent
- Hover: #1e293b (subtle bg)
- Pressed: #334155
- Text: #94a3b8
- Disabled: #64748b (even lighter gray)

Destructive:
- Background: #ef4444
- Hover: #dc2626
- Pressed: #b91c1c
- Disabled: #ef4444 at 40% opacity
```

## ğŸ¯ Icons in Buttons:

You have "Analyze Parlay â†’" with an arrow. Here's how to handle icons:

### **Icon Right** (Like yours)
```
[Text] [Icon]
"Analyze Parlay" â†’
```
**Use for:** Navigation, forward actions

### **Icon Left**
```
[Icon] [Text]
+ "Add to Betslip"
```
**Use for:** Actions that add/create

### **Icon Only**
```
[Icon]
ğŸ” or âœ•
```
**Use for:** Compact spaces, obvious actions

markdown## Buttons

### Primary (Main Actions)
- **Use**: Main CTAs, important actions
- **Background**: #0EA5E9 (bright blue)
- **Text**: White, Bold
- **Sizes**: 48px (large), 40px (medium), 32px (small)
- **Radius**: 12px
- **Examples**: "Analyze Parlay", "Get Started"

### Secondary (Alternative Actions)
- **Use**: Less important actions, alternative options
- **Background**: #334155 (dark slate)
- **Text**: White, Medium weight
- **Sizes**: Same as primary
- **Examples**: "Add to Betslip", "Save"

### Ghost (Tertiary Actions)
- **Use**: Cancel, close, subtle actions
- **Background**: Transparent
- **Text**: #94a3b8 (gray)
- **Hover**: Subtle background #1e293b
- **Examples**: "Cancel", "Close", "Skip"

### Destructive (Dangerous Actions)
- **Use**: Delete, remove, dangerous actions
- **Background**: #ef4444 (red)
- **Text**: White, Bold
- **Examples**: "Delete Betslip", "Clear All"

### States
- **Hover**: Slightly darker shade
- **Disabled**: 40% opacity, not clickable
- **Loading**: Spinner replaces text (or spinner + text)
```

## ğŸ’¡ Gradient Best Practices:

### **DO:**
âœ… Use gradient on primary CTAs
âœ… Keep gradient angle consistent (135deg)
âœ… Use subtle color transition (not too dramatic)
âœ… Add subtle shadow for depth

### **DON'T:**
âŒ Use too many different gradients
âŒ Make gradient too intense (hurts readability)
âŒ Use gradient on every button (dilutes impact)
âŒ Use gradient on text (hard to read)

## ğŸ’¡ Pro Tip: The 98% Scale Trick

On mobile, when user presses button:
```
Scale: 98% (slightly smaller)
Transition: 100ms
This gives tactile feedback that the button was pressed. Way better than hover!
cssbutton:active {
  transform: scale(0.98);
  transition: transform 100ms;
}
Cursor will handle this easily in React!

Ghost/Medium - Cancel, Close
Destructive/Medium - Delete actions (create later if needed)

Keep it simple! You can add more variants later if needed.

```

#### **Medium Buttons:**

```

**If it's disabled state**, you don't need it as separate component - just add opacity to filled button in code.

markdown# Parlays for Days - Design System

Last updated: November 3, 2024

---

## Overview

Parlays for Days is a mobile-first sports betting analysis app with a dark, professional aesthetic emphasizing AI-powered insights. This design system ensures consistency across all screens and components.

---

## Colors

### Primary Palette
- **Primary Blue**: `#0EA5E9` - Main brand color, CTAs
- **Deep Blue**: `#3b82f6` - Gradient endpoint, depth
- **Background**: `#0f172a` - App background (dark navy)
- **Card Background**: `#1e293b` - Card surfaces (dark slate)
- **Card Selected**: `#1e3a5f` - Selected state (lighter slate with blue tint)

### Text Colors
- **Primary Text**: `#ffffff` - Headings, main content
- **Secondary Text**: `#94a3b8` - Subtext, labels, descriptions
- **Tertiary Text**: `#64748b` - Subtle text, disabled states

### Semantic Colors
- **Success (Win)**: `#22c55e` - Green for wins, positive actions
- **Warning (Alert)**: `#f59e0b` - Amber for warnings, upsets
- **Error (Loss)**: `#ef4444` - Red for losses, destructive actions
- **Info**: `#0EA5E9` - Blue for informational elements

### Gradients
- **Primary Button Gradient**: 
  - Angle: 135deg (diagonal)
  - Start: `#0EA5E9`
  - End: `#3b82f6`
- **Pressed State**: Darker gradient
  - Start: `#0284c7`
  - End: `#2563eb`

### Border Colors
- **Default**: `#334155` - Subtle borders
- **Selected**: `#0EA5E9` - Active/selected state
- **Focus**: `#0EA5E9` - Input focus

---

## Typography

### Font Family
- **Primary**: SF Pro Display (iOS native)
- **Fallback**: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, "Segoe UI", system-ui

### Font Sizes & Weights

#### Headings
- **H1 (Screen Titles)**: 24px, Bold (700), White
- **H2 (Section Headers)**: 18px, Bold (700), White  
- **H3 (Card Titles)**: 16px, Bold (700), White

#### Body Text
- **Body Large**: 16px, Regular (400), White
- **Body Medium**: 16px, Medium (500), White
- **Body Small**: 14px, Regular (400), Gray (#94a3b8)

#### UI Elements
- **Button Text**: 16px (large), 14px (medium), Bold (700)
- **Badge Text**: 12px, Medium (500)
- **Caption**: 12px, Regular (400), Gray (#64748b)
- **Tiny**: 10px, Regular (400), Gray (#64748b)

### Line Height
- **Headings**: 1.2 (tight)
- **Body**: 1.5 (comfortable reading)
- **UI Elements**: 1.0 (compact)

---

## Spacing System

### Base Unit: 4px

#### Standard Spacing
- **4px** (xs): Tight spacing, badges
- **8px** (sm): Element spacing within components
- **12px** (md): Between related elements
- **16px** (lg): Component padding, screen margins
- **24px** (xl): Section spacing
- **32px** (2xl): Major section breaks
- **48px** (3xl): Large gutters

#### Specific Uses
- **Screen Padding**: 16px horizontal
- **Card Padding**: 16px all sides
- **Card Margin**: 12px between cards
- **Button Padding**: 16px horizontal, 12px vertical
- **Section Spacing**: 24px between major sections

---

## Border Radius

### Standard Radii
- **Small**: 6px - Badges, tiny elements
- **Medium**: 8px - Buttons (secondary)
- **Large**: 12px - Cards, primary buttons
- **Pill**: 20px - Compact buttons, pills
- **Circle**: 50% - Icons, avatars

---

## Shadows

### Elevation Levels
- **None**: Most cards (flat design)
- **Subtle**: `0 2px 8px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1)` - Floating elements
- **Medium**: `0 4px 12px rgba(14, 165, 233, 0.3)` - Primary buttons
- **Strong**: `0 8px 24px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.2)` - Modals, overlays

---

## Components

### Bottom Navigation

**Specifications:**
- Height: 80px
- Background: `#0f172a` (matches app background)
- Border top: 1px solid `#334155`
- 3 tabs: Home, Betslips, Profile
- Icon size: 24px
- Text: 12px, Medium

**States:**
- **Active**: Blue icon (`#0EA5E9`) + Blue text + Blue indicator
- **Inactive**: Gray icon (`#64748b`) + Gray text

---

### Match Card

**Specifications:**
- Background: `#1e293b`
- Border radius: 12px
- Padding: 16px
- Height: Auto (min 120px)

**Elements:**
- Checkbox: 20px, top-left
- League icon: 24px, left of time
- Time badge: Center-top
- Team logos: 32px
- Analyze button (P4Ds logo): 32px, top-right
- Odds: 16px, right-aligned

**States:**
- **Default**: `#334155` border (1px)
- **Selected**: `#0EA5E9` border (2px), checkbox checked
- **Pressed**: Scale 98%, transition 100ms

---

### Parlay Card

**Specifications:**
- Background: `#1e293b`
- Border radius: 12px
- Padding: 16px
- Margin: 12px between cards

**Variants:**
- ğŸŸ¢ **SAFEST PARLAY**: Green badge (`#22c55e`)
- ğŸŸ¡ **VALUE UPSET PARLAY**: Amber badge (`#f59e0b`)
- ğŸ”µ **BTTS SPECIAL**: Blue badge (`#0EA5E9`)
- ğŸŸ¢ **CONSERVATIVE WIN**: Green badge (`#22c55e`)

**Elements:**
- Badge: Top-left, 12px text
- Odds: Top-right, large (24px)
- Confidence: Below odds, 14px
- Bet legs: 16px, with odds right-aligned
- "Why this works": 14px, gray text
- Button: Full-width at bottom

---

### Buttons

#### Primary Buttons (Gradient)
**Background:**
- Gradient: 135deg, `#0EA5E9` â†’ `#3b82f6`
- Text: White, Bold
- Shadow: `0 4px 12px rgba(14, 165, 233, 0.3)`

**Sizes:**
- **Large**: 48px height, 100% width, 12px radius
- **Medium**: 44px height, 280px width, 12px radius  
- **Compact**: 40px height, auto width, 20px radius (pill)

**States:**
- **Pressed**: Darker gradient + scale 98%
- **Disabled**: 40% opacity, not clickable

**Use Cases:**
- Large: "Analyze matches", "Get Started"
- Medium: "Analyze Parlay"
- Compact: Floating button with icon

---

#### Secondary Buttons (Solid)
**Background:**
- Solid: `#334155`
- Text: White, Medium (500)
- No shadow

**Sizes:**
- Same as primary (48px, 44px, 40px)

**States:**
- **Pressed**: `#475569` + scale 98%
- **Disabled**: 40% opacity

**Use Cases:**
- "Add to Betslip", "Save", alternative actions

---

#### Ghost Buttons (Transparent)
**Background:**
- Transparent
- Text: Gray (`#94a3b8`), Medium
- Border: Optional 1px `#475569`

**States:**
- **Pressed**: Background `#1e293b`, scale 98%

**Use Cases:**
- "Cancel", "Close", "Skip"

---

#### Destructive Buttons (Red)
**Background:**
- Solid: `#ef4444`
- Text: White, Bold
- No shadow

**States:**
- **Pressed**: `#dc2626` + scale 98%

**Use Cases:**
- "Delete Betslip", "Remove", dangerous actions

---

### Form Indicator (W/L/D Circles)

**Specifications:**
- Size: 24px diameter circles
- Spacing: 4px between circles
- Shows last 5 results

**Colors:**
- **Win**: `#22c55e` (green)
- **Loss**: `#ef4444` (red)
- **Draw**: `#64748b` (gray)

---

### Badges

#### Confidence Badge
- Background: `#0EA5E9` (40% opacity)
- Text: White, 12px, Medium
- Padding: 6px 12px
- Radius: 6px
- Icon: ğŸ¤– (optional)

#### Odds Badge
- Background: Transparent
- Text: `#0EA5E9` (positive) or `#ef4444` (negative)
- Font: 16px, Medium
- Format: American (+200, -150)

---

### Floating Button

**Specifications:**
- Position: Fixed bottom, 16px from bottom nav
- Width: Calc(100% - 32px)
- Height: 56px
- Background: `#1e293b`
- Border: 1px solid `#0EA5E9`
- Shadow: `0 8px 24px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3)`

**Content:**
- Left: "X matches selected" (14px, gray)
- Right: "Analyze Parlay â†’" button (gradient, compact)

---

## Mobile-Specific Considerations

### Touch Targets
- Minimum: 44px Ã— 44px
- Preferred: 48px Ã— 48px
- Spacing between targets: 8px minimum

### States (No Hover!)
- **Default**: Normal appearance
- **Pressed**: Scale 98%, darker color, 100ms transition
- **Disabled**: 40% opacity, not tappable
- **Loading**: Spinner replaces content

### Safe Areas
- Respect top safe area (notch/island)
- Bottom nav: 80px + safe area inset
- Screen padding: 16px sides

### Gestures
- Tap: Primary interaction
- Long press: Optional secondary actions
- Swipe: For dismissing cards/modals (future)

---

## Animations & Transitions

### Button Interactions
```css
button:active {
  transform: scale(0.98);
  transition: transform 100ms ease;
}
```

### Card Selection
```css
.card-selected {
  border-color: #0EA5E9;
  transition: border-color 200ms ease;
}
```

### Tooltip Appearance
```css
.tooltip {
  opacity: 0;
  animation: fadeIn 300ms ease forwards;
}
```

### Screen Transitions
- Duration: 200-300ms
- Easing: ease-in-out
- Type: Slide or fade

---

## Accessibility

### Contrast Ratios
- White on dark navy: 15.5:1 (AAA)
- Gray text on dark navy: 7:1 (AA)
- Blue on dark navy: 8.5:1 (AAA)

### Text Sizing
- Minimum body text: 14px
- Minimum button text: 14px
- Important info: 16px+

### Touch Targets
- All interactive elements: 44px minimum
- Clear tap states with scale feedback

---

## Grid & Layout

### Mobile Grid
- Columns: 1 (single column layout)
- Margins: 16px left/right
- Gutters: 12px between cards

### Vertical Rhythm
- Base: 8px
- Major sections: 24px spacing
- Card stacks: 12px spacing

---

## Icons

### Sizes
- Small: 16px (inline with text)
- Medium: 24px (nav, headers)
- Large: 32px (features, logos)

### Style
- Line icons preferred
- 2px stroke weight
- Rounded corners
- Color matches context

### Sources
- System icons (SF Symbols on iOS)
- Custom P4Ds logo
- League logos (32px)
- Team logos (32px-48px)

---

## Loading States

### Spinner
- Size: 32px
- Color: `#0EA5E9`
- Animation: Smooth rotation
- Text below: "Analyzing matches..." (14px, gray)

### Skeleton Screens
- Background: `#1e293b`
- Shimmer: `#334155` â†’ `#475569`
- Animation: 1.5s ease-in-out infinite

---

## Empty States

### Structure
- Icon: 48px, gray
- Heading: 18px, bold, white
- Subtext: 14px, regular, gray
- Button: Primary/large
- Centered vertically and horizontally

### Icons
- ğŸ“‹ Empty clipboard: No betslips
- âš ï¸ Warning: Error states
- ğŸ” Magnifying glass: No results

---

## Error States

### Structure
- Icon: âš ï¸ (red, 48px)
- Heading: "Unable to load matches"
- Subtext: "Check your connection..."
- Primary button: "Retry"
- Ghost button: "Close"

### Tone
- Calm, not alarming
- Clear, actionable guidance
- No technical jargon

---

## Data Formats

### Odds Display
- American format default: +200, -150
- Toggle to Decimal: 2.50, 1.67
- Always prefixed with + or -

### Time Display
- Match time: "TODAY 15:00", "Tomorrow 18:30"
- Saved time: "Oct 30, 3:42 PM"
- Relative: "2 hours ago"

### Confidence Levels
- Display as percentage: 72%
- Color coded: >70% green, 50-70% blue, <50% amber

---

## Platform-Specific Notes

### iOS
- Use SF Pro font (native)
- Respect safe areas (notch, home indicator)
- Native share sheet for sharing
- Haptic feedback on button press

### Android
- Use Roboto font (fallback)
- Material ripple effect on press
- Android share sheet
- Material motion principles

### Web (Future)
- Responsive: 320px minimum
- Desktop: Max width 480px, centered
- Mouse: Add hover states
- Keyboard: Focus indicators

---

Purpose: Explains how components behave and interact (the "how" vs design-system.md's "what")
Copy Everything Below:
markdown# Parlays for Days - Component Behaviors & Notes

Last updated: November 3, 2024

---

## Overview

This document describes how components behave, interact, and handle user actions. Use this alongside design-system.md when building.

---

## Navigation

### Bottom Navigation Bar

**Behavior:**
- Always visible at bottom of screen (fixed position)
- Persists across all screens
- Active tab highlighted with blue color + indicator
- Tap switches between screens instantly (no loading)

**States:**
- **Home**: Match list view
- **Betslips**: Saved/active parlays library
- **Profile**: Settings and preferences

**Interaction:**
- Tap any tab to navigate
- Active tab shows blue icon + text
- Inactive tabs show gray
- No animation between tabs (instant switch)

**Implementation Notes:**
- Fixed bottom position (80px height + safe area)
- Z-index above content but below modals
- Should not scroll with content

---

## Cards

### Match Card

**Default State:**
- Gray border (1px, #334155)
- Checkbox unchecked
- All elements visible

**Selection Flow:**
1. User taps anywhere on card (entire card is tappable)
2. Checkbox animates to checked
3. Border changes to blue (2px, #0EA5E9)
4. Card scales to 98% momentarily (100ms)
5. Floating button appears when 2+ cards selected

**Analyze Button (P4Ds Logo):**
- Top-right corner of card
- 32px touchable area (44px minimum touch target)
- Tap navigates to Single Match Analysis screen
- Does NOT select the card
- Independent action from card selection

**Edge Cases:**
- User can select card AND analyze separately
- Analyze works even if card not selected
- Max selection: No limit (but recommend 5-7 for UX)

**Data Requirements:**
- Team names, logos
- Match time, league
- Current odds (home/away/draw)
- League icon

---

### Parlay Card (Recommendations)

**Types:**
1. **SAFEST PARLAY** (Green badge, high confidence 70%+)
2. **VALUE UPSET PARLAY** (Amber badge, medium confidence 40-60%)
3. **BTTS SPECIAL** (Blue badge, specialized bet type)
4. **CONSERVATIVE WIN** (Green badge, lowest odds, highest confidence)

**Structure:**
- Badge with type (top-left)
- Odds (top-right, large)
- Confidence percentage (below odds)
- List of bet legs with individual odds
- Combined odds (emphasized)
- "Why this works" reasoning (2-3 sentences)
- "Add to Betslip" button (full-width at bottom)

**Interactions:**
- Entire card is NOT tappable (only button is)
- "Add to Betslip" button adds parlay to saved betslips
- Can add multiple parlays to compare
- No visual change after adding (button doesn't disable)

**Button Behavior:**
- Tap "Add to Betslip"
- Show toast notification: "Added to Betslip âœ“"
- Betslip tab badge updates with count
- User stays on current screen
- Can continue browsing

---

## Buttons

### Primary Buttons

**Visual Feedback:**
- **Tap down**: Scale to 98%, gradient darkens
- **Release**: Scale back to 100%, execute action
- **Duration**: 100ms transition

**Loading State:**
- Button text replaced with spinner
- Button still has gradient background
- Button disabled (not tappable)
- Spinner color: white

**Disabled State:**
- 40% opacity
- Not tappable
- No visual feedback on press
- Cursor: not-allowed (web only)

**Text Behavior:**
- Text should be concise: 1-3 words
- No text wrapping (single line)
- Truncate with ellipsis if too long

---

### Secondary Buttons

**Same behavior as primary but:**
- Solid background instead of gradient
- Slightly less emphasis visually

---

### Ghost Buttons

**Visual Feedback:**
- **Tap down**: Background appears (#1e293b), scale 98%
- **Release**: Background fades out, execute action

**Use Cases:**
- "Cancel" in modals
- "Close" in overlays
- "Skip" in onboarding

---

### Floating Button (Analyze Parlay)

**Appearance:**
- Appears when 2+ match cards selected
- Slides up from bottom (300ms animation)
- Positioned above bottom nav, with 16px gap
- Persists while scrolling

**Content:**
- Left side: "X matches selected" (dynamic count)
- Right side: "Analyze Parlay â†’" button (gradient)

**Interactions:**
- Tap button (not entire bar) to analyze
- Navigates to Parlay Analysis screen
- Passes selected match IDs to next screen
- Selection state persists if user goes back

**Dismissal:**
- Deselect all cards: Button slides down and disappears
- User navigates away: Button disappears
- User completes parlay analysis: Selection clears

---

## Interactive Elements

### Checkboxes (Match Selection)

**States:**
- Unchecked: Empty square, gray border
- Checked: Blue background, white checkmark
- Disabled: Gray, 40% opacity

**Behavior:**
- Tap checkbox to toggle
- Tap anywhere on card also toggles checkbox
- Animate check/uncheck (200ms)

---

### Toggle Switches

**Usage:**
- Odds format (American/Decimal)
- Notifications (On/Off)

**Behavior:**
- Tap to toggle instantly
- No confirmation needed
- Save preference to local storage
- Haptic feedback on toggle (mobile)

---

### Form Indicator (W/L/D Circles)

**Display:**
- Shows last 5 results (most recent on right)
- Green (W), Red (L), Gray (D)
- 24px circles, 4px spacing
- Left-to-right = oldest to newest

**Interaction:**
- Not tappable
- Static display only
- Tooltip on hover (web only): "Win vs Arsenal"

---

## Screens

### Home Screen

**Initial Load:**
1. Show loading state (spinner)
2. Fetch today's matches
3. Animate matches in (fade up, staggered 50ms)
4. Show tooltip on first load (pointing to P4Ds logo)

**Scroll Behavior:**
- Vertical scroll only
- Header (logo) sticks to top
- Filters stick below header
- Match cards scroll
- Bottom nav always visible

**Pull to Refresh:**
- Pull down from top
- Show loading indicator
- Refresh match data
- Odds updated in real-time

---

### Single Match Analysis

**Entry:**
- Tap P4Ds logo on match card
- Loading screen: "Analyzing matches..."
- Duration: 5-15 seconds (API call)
- Then show full analysis

**Content:**
- All sections expanded by default
- Scroll to see all information
- No back button needed (use system back)

**Sections:**
- League Position
- Recent Form
- Injuries & Suspensions
- Head-to-Head
- Key Stats
- Top Scorers
- Referee Info
- Fouls & Cards
- Advanced Stats

**Exit:**
- System back button returns to home
- Match card remains in same state (selected/unselected)

---

### Parlay Analysis

**Entry:**
- From floating "Analyze Parlay" button
- Loading screen: "Analyzing matches..."
- Duration: 10-30 seconds (multiple matches)
- Then show full parlay analysis

**Match Breakdown:**
- Collapsible sections (tap to expand/collapse)
- First match expanded by default
- Chevron indicates expand/collapse state
- Smooth animation (300ms)

**Recommendations:**
- All 4 parlay cards visible
- Scroll vertically to see all
- Can add multiple to betslips
- Each addition shows toast notification

**Upset Alerts:**
- Yellow/Red badges
- Highlight high-risk, high-reward bets
- Optional to consider

**Top Individual Bets:**
- For users who don't want parlays
- Single bet recommendations
- Tap to add to betslip (future feature)

---

### Betslips Library

**Tabs:**
- **Active**: Upcoming matches, bets not yet placed
- **Saved**: Past analyses, historical parlays

**Filter Behavior:**
- Tap tab to switch instantly
- Content updates with fade transition (200ms)
- Empty state if no betslips in that category

**Betslip Cards:**
- Show parlay name, teams, odds, confidence
- Tap card to view full details (future)
- Swipe to delete (future)
- Actions: View, Share, Delete

**Empty State:**
- Shows when no betslips in selected tab
- Icon, text, button to analyze matches
- Button navigates to home screen

---

### Profile/Settings

**Sections:**
- Settings (odds format, notifications)
- Help & Support (FAQ, contact, about)
- Footer (version number)

**Settings Changes:**
- Toggle switches save immediately
- No "Save" button needed
- Changes reflected app-wide instantly

**Navigation:**
- Tap row with chevron to go to detail screen
- Back button returns to profile

---

## Loading States

**When to Show:**
- Initial app load
- Analyzing matches (single or parlay)
- Fetching odds data
- Saving betslip

**What to Show:**
- Centered spinner (32px, blue)
- Text below: "Analyzing matches..."
- Dark background
- Bottom nav still visible

**Duration:**
- Target: <5 seconds for single match
- Target: <15 seconds for parlay
- Show timeout error after 30 seconds

---

## Error States

**When to Show:**
- Network failure
- API timeout
- No matches available
- Invalid data

**Structure:**
- Warning icon (âš ï¸, red, 48px)
- Clear error message
- Actionable guidance
- "Retry" button (primary)
- "Close" button (ghost) optional

**Error Messages:**
- "Unable to load matches" + "Check your connection"
- "Something went wrong" + "We're looking into it"
- "No matches available" + "Check back soon"

**User Actions:**
- Retry: Attempt action again
- Close: Return to previous screen
- Contact Support: Open support (future)

---

## Empty States

**Variations:**

**No Betslips:**
- Icon: ğŸ“‹ (48px, gray)
- Text: "No saved parlays"
- Subtext: "Analyze matches to save your first parlay"
- Button: "Analyze Matches" â†’ Home screen

**No Search Results:**
- Icon: ğŸ” (48px, gray)
- Text: "No matches found"
- Subtext: "Try different filters"
- Button: "Clear Filters"

**No Matches Today:**
- Icon: ğŸ“… (48px, gray)
- Text: "No matches today"
- Subtext: "Check back tomorrow"
- Button: "View Upcoming"

---

## Tooltips & Onboarding

### First Load Tooltip

**Trigger:**
- First time user opens app
- Stored in localStorage: "tooltipSeen"

**Behavior:**
1. App loads normally
2. After 500ms delay, tooltip appears
3. Points to P4Ds logo on first match card
4. Text: "Tap for AI analysis"
5. Auto-dismisses after 3 seconds
6. OR user taps anywhere to dismiss
7. Never shows again

**Visual:**
- White background
- Black text (14px)
- Blue arrow pointing to logo
- Subtle shadow
- Rounded corners (8px)

---

### Onboarding (Optional Future)

**Screens:**
1. Welcome: App name, tagline, continue
2. How it works: Tap logo for analysis
3. Get started: Navigate to home

**Behavior:**
- Skippable at any point
- Only shows once
- Stored in localStorage: "onboardingComplete"

---

## Data Updates

### Real-Time Odds

**Update Frequency:**
- Poll API every 30 seconds when app is open
- Only update changed odds
- Show subtle flash animation on change

**Visual Indicator:**
- Odds briefly flash blue when updated
- No intrusive notifications

---

### Live Match Updates

**During Match:**
- Show "LIVE" badge on card
- Update score in real-time
- Red pulsing indicator

**Post-Match:**
- Show final score
- Mark betslip as "Completed" (if outcome tracking added)

---

## Animations

### Card Selection
```
Duration: 200ms
Easing: ease-out
Effect: Border color change + scale 98%
```

### Screen Transitions
```
Duration: 300ms
Easing: ease-in-out
Effect: Fade or slide
```

### Tooltip Appearance
```
Duration: 300ms
Easing: ease-out
Effect: Fade in + slide up slightly
```

### Button Press
```
Duration: 100ms
Easing: ease
Effect: Scale 98%
```

### Toast Notifications
```
Duration: 250ms in, 2000ms visible, 250ms out
Easing: ease-in-out
Effect: Slide up from bottom
```

---

## Persistence & Storage

### Local Storage
- Tooltip seen: Boolean
- Onboarding complete: Boolean
- Odds format preference: "american" | "decimal"
- Notifications enabled: Boolean
- Selected matches: Array of match IDs (cleared on parlay analysis)

### Database (Supabase)
- Saved betslips
- User preferences (if authenticated)
- Analysis history

---

## API Integration Notes

### The Odds API
- Endpoint: Get today's matches by sport/league
- Rate limit: 500 requests/month (free tier)
- Poll frequency: Every 30 seconds when app open
- Cache: 30 seconds

### API-Football
- Endpoint: Match details, stats, injuries
- Used for: Form data, H2H, injuries, standings
- Rate limit: Based on plan
- Cache: Match data (1 hour), injuries (15 min)

### Claude API (AI Analysis)
- Trigger: User taps analyze
- Input: Match data + context
- Output: JSON with analysis
- Average duration: 5-10 seconds
- Cost: ~$0.01-0.03 per analysis

---

## Error Handling

### Network Errors
- Show error state with retry
- Log to error tracking (future: Sentry)
- Provide fallback: cached data if available

### API Rate Limits
- Show user-friendly message: "Too many requests, try again soon"
- Implement exponential backoff

### Invalid Data
- Validate all API responses
- Show error if data malformed
- Log to error tracking

---

## Performance Considerations

### Image Loading
- Lazy load team logos
- Use CDN for logos (API-Football CDN)
- Fallback: Show team initials if logo fails

### Data Fetching
- Fetch today's matches on app open
- Cache for 30 seconds
- Pagination if >20 matches

### Analysis Generation
- Show loading state during API call
- Don't block UI
- Allow user to navigate away (cancel in background)

---

## Accessibility (Future Considerations)

### Screen Readers
- All buttons have labels
- Images have alt text
- Cards have accessible names

### Text Scaling
- Support iOS dynamic type
- Test at 200% scale

### Color Blindness
- Don't rely solely on color (use icons + text)
- W/L/D: Green/Red/Gray + letters

---

## Future Features (Not in MVP)

- User authentication
- Bet outcome tracking
- Win/loss statistics
- Bet history analytics
- Social sharing with friends
- Push notifications for lineup news
- Live match tracking
- More sports (NFL, NBA, etc.)
- Dark/light theme toggle
- Multiple language support

---

Purpose: Overview of the project for developers (or future you!)
Copy Everything Below:
markdown# Parlays for Days

**AI-Powered Sports Betting Analysis App**

---

## Overview

Parlays for Days is a mobile-first web application that provides comprehensive, AI-powered analysis for sports betting. Built with Next.js and powered by Claude AI, it helps users make informed betting decisions by analyzing team form, injuries, statistics, and historical data.

---

## Features

### Core Functionality
- ğŸ“Š **AI Match Analysis**: Deep dive into any match with AI-generated insights
- ğŸ¯ **Smart Parlay Builder**: Build multi-match parlays with AI confidence ratings
- ğŸ“ˆ **Real-Time Odds**: Live odds from major sportsbooks
- ğŸ¥ **Injury Reports**: Up-to-date player injury and suspension tracking
- ğŸ“‹ **Betslip Management**: Save and organize your analysis for future reference
- ğŸ¤– **AI Pick of the Day**: Daily curated recommendation

### Design Philosophy
- Mobile-first, responsive design
- Dark theme with professional aesthetic
- Fast, intuitive user experience
- No clutter, just actionable insights

---

## Tech Stack

### Frontend
- **Framework**: Next.js 14 (App Router)
- **Language**: TypeScript
- **Styling**: Tailwind CSS
- **Components**: React functional components with hooks

### Backend & Data
- **Database**: Supabase (PostgreSQL)
- **APIs**:
  - The Odds API (live odds, match data)
  - API-Football (stats, injuries, form)
  - Claude API (AI analysis via Anthropic)

### Deployment
- **Hosting**: Vercel
- **Analytics**: (TBD: Mixpanel or Amplitude)
- **Error Tracking**: (TBD: Sentry)

---

â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ lib/              # Utilities and helpers

```

---

## Getting Started

### Prerequisites
- Node.js 18+ 
- npm or yarn
- API keys for:
  - The Odds API
  - API-Football
  - Claude API (Anthropic)
  - Supabase project

### Installation
```bash
# Clone repository
git clone https://github.com/yourusername/parlays-for-days.git

# Navigate to project
cd parlays-for-days

# Install dependencies
npm install

# Set up environment variables
cp .env.example .env.local
# Add your API keys to .env.local

# Run development server
npm run dev
```

Open [http://localhost:3000](http://localhost:3000) in your browser.

---

## Environment Variables

Create a `.env.local` file:
```env
# APIs
ODDS_API_KEY=your_odds_api_key
API_FOOTBALL_KEY=your_api_football_key
ANTHROPIC_API_KEY=your_claude_api_key

# Database
NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL=your_supabase_url
NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY=your_supabase_anon_key

# Optional
NEXT_PUBLIC_APP_URL=http://localhost:3000
```

- Color palette
- Typography
- Spacing system
- Component specifications
- Mobile interaction patterns

## Development Workflow

### Running Locally
```bash
npm run dev          # Start dev server
npm run build        # Build for production
npm run start        # Start production server
npm run lint         # Run ESLint
```

### Component Development
1. Check `component-library.png` for design reference
2. Build component following design-system.md specs
3. Test on mobile viewport (375px width)
4. Verify interactions match component-notes.md

---

## Key Components

### Navigation
- `BottomNav`: Fixed navigation bar (Home, Betslips, Profile)

### Cards
- `MatchCard`: Individual match with selection and analysis
- `ParlayCard`: AI-generated parlay recommendations

### Buttons
- `PrimaryButton`: Main actions with gradient
- `SecondaryButton`: Alternative actions
- `GhostButton`: Tertiary actions
- `FloatingButton`: Appears on multi-select

### Screens
- `HomePage`: Match list with filters
- `SingleMatchAnalysis`: Deep dive on one match
- `ParlayAnalysis`: Multi-match parlay breakdown
- `BetslipsLibrary`: Saved analyses

---

## API Integration

### The Odds API
```typescript
// Fetch today's matches
GET https://api.the-odds-api.com/v4/sports/{sport}/odds
```

### API-Football
```typescript
// Get match statistics
GET https://v3.football.api-sports.io/fixtures/statistics
```

### Claude API (Anthropic)
```typescript
// Generate AI analysis
POST https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages
```

See `/lib/api/` for wrapper functions.

---

## Deployment

### Vercel (Recommended)
```bash
# Install Vercel CLI
npm i -g vercel

# Deploy
vercel

# Production deployment
vercel --prod
```

### Environment Variables
Add all `.env.local` variables to Vercel project settings.

markdown# Parlays for Days

**AI-Powered Sports Betting Analysis App**

---

## Overview

Parlays for Days is a mobile-first web application that provides comprehensive, AI-powered analysis for sports betting. Built with Next.js and powered by Claude AI, it helps users make informed betting decisions by analyzing team form, injuries, statistics, and historical data.

---

## Features

### Core Functionality
- ğŸ“Š **AI Match Analysis**: Deep dive into any match with AI-generated insights
- ğŸ¯ **Smart Parlay Builder**: Build multi-match parlays with AI confidence ratings
- ğŸ“ˆ **Real-Time Odds**: Live odds from major sportsbooks
- ğŸ¥ **Injury Reports**: Up-to-date player injury and suspension tracking
- ğŸ“‹ **Betslip Management**: Save and organize your analysis for future reference
- ğŸ¤– **AI Pick of the Day**: Daily curated recommendation

### Design Philosophy
- Mobile-first, responsive design
- Dark theme with professional aesthetic
- Fast, intuitive user experience
- No clutter, just actionable insights

---

## Tech Stack

### Frontend
- **Framework**: Next.js 14 (App Router)
- **Language**: TypeScript
- **Styling**: Tailwind CSS
- **Components**: React functional components with hooks

### Backend & Data
- **Database**: Supabase (PostgreSQL)
- **APIs**:
  - The Odds API (live odds, match data)
  - API-Football (stats, injuries, form)
  - Claude API (AI analysis via Anthropic)

### Deployment
- **Hosting**: Vercel
- **Analytics**: (TBD)
- **Error Tracking**: (TBD)

---

## Getting Started

### Prerequisites
- Node.js 18+ 
- npm or yarn
- API keys for:
  - The Odds API
  - API-Football
  - Claude API (Anthropic)
  - Supabase project

### Installation
```bash
# Clone repository
git clone https://github.com/yourusername/parlays-for-days.git

# Navigate to project
cd parlays-for-days

# Install dependencies
npm install

# Set up environment variables
cp .env.example .env.local
# Add your API keys to .env.local

# Run development server
npm run dev
```

Open [http://localhost:3000](http://localhost:3000) in your browser.

---

## Environment Variables

Create a `.env.local` file:
```env
# APIs
ODDS_API_KEY=your_odds_api_key
API_FOOTBALL_KEY=your_api_football_key
ANTHROPIC_API_KEY=your_claude_api_key

# Database
NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL=your_supabase_url
NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY=your_supabase_anon_key

# Optional
NEXT_PUBLIC_APP_URL=http://localhost:3000
```

---

## Design System

See [design-system.md](./design-system.md) for comprehensive design guidelines including:
- Color palette
- Typography
- Spacing system
- Component specifications
- Mobile interaction patterns

See [component-notes.md](./component-notes.md) for component behaviors and interactions.

---

## Development Workflow

### Running Locally
```bash
npm run dev          # Start dev server
npm run build        # Build for production
npm run start        # Start production server
npm run lint         # Run ESLint
```

### Component Development
1. Check `component-library.png` for design reference
2. Build component following design-system.md specs
3. Test on mobile viewport (375px width)
4. Verify interactions match component-notes.md

---

## Key Components

### Navigation
- `BottomNav`: Fixed navigation bar (Home, Betslips, Profile)

### Cards
- `MatchCard`: Individual match with selection and analysis
- `ParlayCard`: AI-generated parlay recommendations

### Buttons
- `PrimaryButton`: Main actions with gradient
- `SecondaryButton`: Alternative actions
- `GhostButton`: Tertiary actions
- `FloatingButton`: Appears on multi-select

### Screens
- `HomePage`: Match list with filters
- `SingleMatchAnalysis`: Deep dive on one match
- `ParlayAnalysis`: Multi-match parlay breakdown
- `BetslipsLibrary`: Saved analyses

---

## API Integration

### The Odds API
```typescript
// Fetch today's matches
GET https://api.the-odds-api.com/v4/sports/{sport}/odds
```

### API-Football
```typescript
// Get match statistics
GET https://v3.football.api-sports.io/fixtures/statistics
```

### Claude API (Anthropic)
```typescript
// Generate AI analysis
POST https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages
```

See `/lib/api/` for wrapper functions.

---

## Deployment

### Vercel (Recommended)
```bash
# Install Vercel CLI
npm i -g vercel

# Deploy
vercel

# Production deployment
vercel --prod
```

### Environment Variables
Add all `.env.local` variables to Vercel project settings.

./components/BottomNav.tsx:3:10
Ecmascript file had an error
> 3 | import { usePathname } from "next/navigation";

You're importing a component that needs `usePathname`. This React Hook only works in a Client Component. To fix, mark the file (or its parent) with the "use client" directive.
This is a common Next.js error. The BottomNav component is using usePathname which is a React hook that only works in client components, but the file isn't marked as a client component.
The fix is simple: Add "use client" at the top of the BottomNav.tsx file.
The server is running (you can see "Ready in 1570ms"), but there's a compilation error preventing the page from loading. It shows "GET / 500 in 2.2s" which means there's a server error.
The user needs to tell Cursor to fix this error.THERE'S AN ERROR - BUT IT'S EASY TO FIX! ğŸ”§

ğŸš¨ What's Wrong:
The error says:
BottomNav.tsx:3:10
You're importing a component that needs `usePathname`. 
This React Hook only works in a Client Component. 
To fix, mark the file with the "use client" directive.
```

**This is a common Next.js issue!** The BottomNav is using React hooks, which need to be marked as a "Client Component."

---

## âœ… How to Fix:

**Tell Cursor:**
```
There's an error in BottomNav.tsx. It needs "use client" at the top of the file.

Please add "use client"; as the first line in:
- components/BottomNav.tsx
- components/MatchCard.tsx (it might need it too)

This will fix the usePathname error.

ğŸ’¡ Why This Happens:
Next.js 14 has two types of components:

Server Components (default) - Can't use hooks
Client Components (need "use client") - Can use hooks like usePathname, useState, etc.

Bottom navigation needs to know which route you're on (usePathname), so it needs to be a client component.

ğŸ¯ After Cursor Fixes It:
The page will refresh automatically and you'll see your app! ğŸ‰

ğŸ’¡ Why Polish is Actually Easy:
Functional Logic vs Visual Polish:
Hard (what you did):
typescript// Complex logic
const [selected, setSelected] = useState([]);
const handleSelect = (id) => {
  setSelected(prev => 
    prev.includes(id) 
      ? prev.filter(x => x !== id) 
      : [...prev, id]
  );
};
This requires thinking, logic, problem-solving.
Easy (polish):
typescript// Just swapping elements
// Before:
<div className="w-8 h-8 bg-white rounded" />

// After:
<img src="/logos/man-city.png" className="w-8 h-8" />
```
**This is literally find-and-replace.**

---

## ğŸ”§ How Polish Works with Cursor:

### **Example: Adding Real Team Logos**

**You say:**
```
The team logos are white boxes. Replace them with actual logos.
Use these placeholder URLs for now:
- Man City: /logos/man-city.png
- Liverpool: /logos/liverpool.png
- Arsenal: /logos/arsenal.png
- Chelsea: /logos/chelsea.png
Cursor does:
typescript// Changes this:
<div className="w-8 h-8 bg-white rounded" />

// To this:
<img 
  src={`/logos/${team.toLowerCase().replace(' ', '-')}.png`}
  alt={team}
  className="w-8 h-8 rounded-full"
/>
```

**Takes 30 seconds.**

---

## ğŸ“‹ Polish Roadmap - Step by Step:

### **Phase 1: Icons (30 min)**
- Bottom nav icons (home, betslips, profile)
- P4Ds logo for analyze button
- League icons (EPL badge)
All from free icon libraries or SVG code

### **Phase 2: Team Logos (30 min)**
- Use API-Football CDN (they provide logos!)
- Or use placeholder service initially
- Cursor can fetch and display automatically

### **Phase 3: Spacing/Alignment (20 min)**
- "Card padding is 14px, should be 16px"
- "Odds should be right-aligned with 8px margin"
- Cursor adjusts instantly

### **Phase 4: Colors/Borders (15 min)**
- "Border should be #334155, currently too bright"
- "Selected state needs 2px border not 1px"
- Simple CSS changes

### **Phase 5: Animations (15 min)**
- Button press scale effect
- Card selection transition
- Smooth scrolling
Optional but nice!

**Total polish time: ~2 hours of actual work**

ğŸ”§ What That "N" Actually Is:

Route information
Turbopack status
Development preferences
Performance metrics

This is ONLY visible in development mode.
When you build and deploy your app (npm run build), this won't exist at all! ğŸ‰

Next.js version: 16.0.1 (Turbopack)Show moreIdentified Next.js image domain configuration requirement and solution.The user is getting a Next.js image configuration error. This is because Next.js requires external image domains to be whitelisted in the next.config.js file for security reasons.
The error is clear: the hostname "media.api-sports.io" needs to be configured in next.config.js under the images configuration.
This is a common Next.js issue and easy to fix. I need to give them a clear message for Cursor to fix this.EASY FIX! This is a Next.js security setting.

ğŸ”§ What Happened:
Next.js requires you to whitelist external image domains for security. Cursor tried to use API-Football's image CDN but it's not configured yet.

ğŸ’¬ Message to Send to Cursor:
There's a Next.js image configuration error. 

The error says: hostname "media.api-sports.io" is not configured under images in next.config.js

Please fix this by:

1. Open next.config.js
2. Add the API-Football image domain to the images configuration:

images: {
  remotePatterns: [
    {
      protocol: 'https',
      hostname: 'media.api-sports.io',
      pathname: '/football/**',
    },
  ],
}

This will allow Next.js to load team badge images from the API-Football CDN.

After making this change, the dev server will need to restart automatically.

â±ï¸ What Will Happen:

Cursor updates next.config.js
Dev server restarts (automatic)
Images load properly
Team badges appear!

This takes ~30 seconds to fix! âœ…

ğŸ’¡ Why This Happens:
Next.js Image Optimization:

Next.js optimizes all images for performance
For security, it only allows approved external domains
You have to explicitly whitelist each image CDN

This is a GOOD thing - it prevents random external images from being loaded.
